        $(window).load(function() {
 		var sblength = $('.col-ps-sidebar').outerHeight();
 		var camplength = $('.col-minor').outerHeight();
                                 if(camplength <= 1)
 		{
 			$('.col-ps-sidebar').hide();
 		}
 		else if(sblength > camplength)
 		{
 			// var widgetlength = $('#skInjectPluginContainer-1').outerHeight();
 			var widgetlength = 477;
 			var sbilength = $('.ps_sidebar-item').outerHeight();
 			var sliceval = Math.floor((camplength-widgetlength)/sbilength);
 			if (sliceval === 0 || sliceval < 0){$('.ps_sidebar-item').slice(1).hide();}
 			else{$('.ps_sidebar-item').slice(sliceval).hide();}
 		}
 	});
       </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var enhancedCommerceHelper = (function () {
 
         var getPageTypeMetadata = function () {
             var listing = "";
             var isCampaignProduct = false;
             if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("markalar") > -1
                 && window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya") == -1) {
                 listing = "Season Brand Listing > " + $("h1").first().text();
             }
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("markalar") == -1 && window.location.pathname.indexOf("marka") > -1
                 && window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya") == -1) {
                 listing = "Season Brand-Category Listing > " + $("h1").first().text();
             }
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya/liste") > -1) {
                 listing = "Campaign Listing > " + $("h1").first().text() + "|" + clientContext.currentCampaign;
                 isCampaignProduct = true;
             }
 
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("liste") > -1) {
                 listing = "Season Category Listing > " + $("h1").first().text();
             }
 
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("sepet") > -1) {
                 listing = "Sepet";
             }
 
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("vitrin") > -1) {
                 listing = "Vitrin > " + $("h1").first().text();
             }
 
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya/arama") > -1) {
                 listing = "Campaign Search Listing > " + $("h1").first().text();
                 isCampaignProduct = true;
             }
 
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("arama") > -1) {
                 listing = "Season Search Listing > " + $("h1").first().text();
             }
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("kategori") > -1) {
                 listing = "Season Virtual Listing > " + $("h1").first().text();
             }
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("siparis-basarili") > -1) {
                 listing = "Sipariş Başarılı";
             }
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya/detay") > -1) {
                 listing = "PS Prod Detail";
             }
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("detay") > -1) {
                 listing = "Season Prod Detail";
             }
             else if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya/alisveris") > -1) {
                 var campaignTypeId = window.location.pathname.slice(-1);
                 switch (campaignTypeId) {
                     case "1":
                         listing = "PS Vitrin > Kadın";
                         break;
                     case "2":
                         listing = "PS Vitrin > Erkek";
                         break;
                     case "3":
                         listing = "PS Vitrin > Çocuk";
                         break;
                     case "4":
                         listing = "PS Vitrin > Ev & Yaşam";
                         break;
                     case "5":
                         listing = "PS Vitrin > Ayakkabı & Çanta";
                         break;
                     case "6":
                         listing = "PS Vitrin > Hızlı Gönderi";
                         break;
                     case "7":
                         listing = "PS Vitrin > Spor Giyim";
                         break;
                     default:
                         listing = "PS Anasayfa";
                         break;
                 }
             }
 
             else
                 listing = "";
             return {
                 listing: listing,
                 isCampaignProduct: isCampaignProduct
             };
         }
 
         var inViewport = function (elem, min_percentage_shown, horizontalConstraintfunc) {
             var $elem = $(elem);
 
             min_percentage_shown = min_percentage_shown || 1;
 
             var elem_height = $elem.height(),
                 elem_top = $elem.offset().top,
                 elem_bottom = elem_top + elem_height,
                 win_top = $(document).scrollTop(),
                 win_bottom = win_top + $(window).height(),
                 top_delta = elem_top - win_top,
                 bottom_delta = win_bottom - elem_bottom,
                 visible_pixels = elem_height +
                                      Math.min(top_delta, 0) +
                                      Math.min(bottom_delta, 0),
                 percentage_shown = visible_pixels / elem_height;
 
             var horizontally_visible = true;
             if (horizontalConstraintfunc) {
                 horizontally_visible = horizontalConstraintfunc($elem);
             }
 
 
             return percentage_shown >= min_percentage_shown && horizontally_visible;
         }
 
         var flushBufferNow = function (impressionDto) {
             impressionDto.flush_buffer_at = +new Date();
             clearInterval(impressionDto.flush_buffer_timeout_id);
             flushBuffer(impressionDto);
         }
 
         var flushBufferLater = function (impressionDto, seconds_delayed) {
             // Cancel if there already is a scheduled flush action,
             if (+new Date() < impressionDto.flush_buffer_at)
                 return;
 
             impressionDto.flush_buffer_at = +new Date() + seconds_delayed * 1000;
 
             impressionDto.flush_buffer_timeout_id =
               setTimeout(function () { flushBuffer(impressionDto) }, seconds_delayed * 1000)
         }
 
         // This func should only be used by "flushBufferNow" and
         // "flushBufferLater". Don't use this directly.
         var flushBuffer = function (impressionDto) {
             var maxItemsPerRequest = 40;
             var exceedingItemCount = impressionDto.buffered_items.length - maxItemsPerRequest;
             if (exceedingItemCount > 0) {
                 var buffer_clone = $.extend([], impressionDto.buffered_items.slice(exceedingItemCount - 1, maxItemsPerRequest + exceedingItemCount - 1)),
                 event = impressionDto.options.imps.event(buffer_clone);
                 impressionDto.buffered_items.length = impressionDto.buffered_items.length - maxItemsPerRequest;
                 flushBufferLater(impressionDto, 2);
             } else {
                 var buffer_clone = $.extend([], impressionDto.buffered_items),
                 event = impressionDto.options.imps.event(buffer_clone);
                 impressionDto.buffered_items.length = 0;
             }
 
             impressionDto.options.push(event);
         }
 
         var registerImpressions = function ($elems, impressionDto) {
             var beginPosition = 0;
             if ($('.bottom-pager li.active a').length > 0) {
                 var pagingSize = parseInt($('#productlist-count').val());
                 var selectedPager = parseInt($('.bottom-pager li.active a').html());
                 beginPosition = pagingSize * (selectedPager - 1);
             }
 
             items = $elems
 
                     // filter out non visible items:
                     .filter(function () {
                         return enhancedCommerceHelper.inViewport(this, impressionDto.options.imps.min_percentage_shown, impressionDto.horizontalConstraintfunc);
                     })
 
 
 
                     // convert items to ee impression item objects:
                     .map(function (idx, elem) {
                         var absolute_idx = beginPosition + $elems.index(elem),
                             relative_idx = idx;
 
 
 
                         return impressionDto.options.imps.item(absolute_idx, elem, relative_idx)
                     })
 
                     // filter out items that has already been reported:
                     .filter(function (idx, item) {
                         return !impressionDto.impressions_sent[item.id];
                     })
 
                     // push items to buffer
                     .each(function (idx, item) {
                         impressionDto.buffered_items.push(item);
                         impressionDto.impressions_sent[item.id] = true;
                         impressionDto.impressions_count += 1;
                     });
 
             if (items.length)
                 flushBufferLater(impressionDto, impressionDto.options.imps.buffer_flush_delay);
         }
 
         var prodImpressionEventDef = function (items) {
             return {
                 Category: 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
                 Action: 'Browse',
                 Label: 'Product Impressions',
                 Value: 0,
                 event: 'eeEvent',
 
                 ecommerce: {
                     currencyCode: 'TRY',
                     impressions: items
                 },
 
                 nonInteraction: true
             }
         };
 
         var promoImpressionEventDef = function (items) {
             return {
                 ecommerce: {
                     promoView: {
                         promotions:items
                     }
                 },
                 Category: 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
                 Action: 'Browse',
                 Label: 'Campaign Impression',
                 noninteraction: true,
                 Value: 0,
                 event: 'eeEvent'
             }
         };
 
         var productClickNativeRecommendation = function (element, listingName) {
             if (element.hasClass("next-con") || element.hasClass("prev-con"))
                 return;
 
             pageTypeMetadata = getPageTypeMetadata();
 
             var clicked_product = [{
                 'id': element.data("productid"),
                 'name': '',
                 'brand': element.data("brand"),
                 'category': '',
                 'dimension13': pageTypeMetadata.isCampaignProduct ? "Campaign Product" : "Season Product",
                 'dimension14': '',
                 'dimension15': '',
                 'position': element.index() + 1
             }];
 
             
             dataLayer.push({
                 'Category': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
                 'Action': 'Browse',
                 'Label': 'Product Click',
                 'Value': 0,
                 'noninteraction': false,
                 'ecommerce': {
                     'click': {
                         'actionField': { 'list': listingName },
                         'products': clicked_product
                     }
                 },
                 'event': 'eeEvent'
             });
         }
 
         var productClickRemovedRecommendation = function (element, listingName) {
       
             if (element.hasClass("next-con") || element.hasClass("prev-con"))
                 return;
 
             pageTypeMetadata = getPageTypeMetadata();            
             var clicked_product = [{
                 'id': element.parents().eq(1).data("productid"),
                 'name': element.parents().eq(1).data("productname"),
                 'brand': element.parents().eq(1).data("brand"),
                 'category': '',
                 'dimension13': element.parents().eq(1).data("iscampaign") ? "Campaign Product" : "Season Product",
                 'dimension14': '',
                 'dimension15': '',
                 'position': element.parents().eq(1).index() + 1
             }];
                         
             dataLayer.push({
                 'Category': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
                 'Action': 'Browse',
                 'Label': 'Product Click',
                 'Value': 0,
                 'noninteraction': false,
                 'ecommerce': {
                     'click': {
                         'actionField': { 'list': listingName },
                         'products': clicked_product
                     }
                 },
                 'event': 'eeEvent'
             });
         }
 
         var productClickSkRecommendation = function (element, listingName,productId) {
             if (!element) {
                 element = $("#sk-carousel-widget li a").filter(function () { return $(this).prop("href").indexOf(productId) > 0 }).parent("li");
             }
             if (element.hasClass("next-con") || element.hasClass("prev-con"))
                 return;
             var dim13 = "";
             var prodId = '';
             var anchor = $(element).find("a");
             var regexGroup = anchor.prop("href").match(/(\d+)\/detay/);
             if (regexGroup == null) {
                 regexGroup = anchor.prop("href").match(/kampanya\/detay\/(\d+)/);
                 dim13 = "Campaign Product";
                 if (regexGroup.length == 2)
                     prodId = regexGroup[1];
             } else {
                 dim13 = "Season Product";
                 if (regexGroup.length == 2)
                     prodId = regexGroup[1];
             }
 
 
 
             pageTypeMetadata = getPageTypeMetadata();
 
             var clicked_product = [{
                 'id': prodId,
                 'name': anchor.find(".brand").html() + " " + anchor.find(".name").html() + "|" + prodId,
                 'brand': anchor.find(".brand").html(),
                 'category': '',
                 'dimension13': dim13,
                 'dimension14': '',
                 'dimension15': '',
                 'position': element.index() + 1
             }];
 
             dataLayer.push({
                 'Category': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
                 'Action': 'Browse',
                 'Label': 'Product Click',
                 'Value': 0,
                 'noninteraction': false,
                 'ecommerce': {
                     'click': {
                         'actionField': { 'list': listingName },
                         'products': clicked_product
                     }
                 },
                 'event': 'eeEvent'
             });
         }
 
         return {
             getPageTypeMetadata: getPageTypeMetadata,
             inViewport: inViewport,
             flushBufferLater: flushBufferLater,
             flushBufferNow: flushBufferNow,
             registerImpressions: registerImpressions,
             prodImpressionEventDef: prodImpressionEventDef,
             promoImpressionEventDef: promoImpressionEventDef,
             productClickNativeRecommendation: productClickNativeRecommendation,
             productClickSkRecommendation: productClickSkRecommendation,
             productClickRemovedRecommendation: productClickRemovedRecommendation
         };
     })();
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    (function () {
         var pageTypeMetadata = enhancedCommerceHelper.getPageTypeMetadata();
 
         function trackLastViewedProducts() {
             var lastViewedProdImpressions = {
                 impressions_count: 0,
                 impressions_sent: {},
                 buffered_items: [],
                 flush_buffer_at: 0,
                 options: {
                     push: function (event) {
                         if (event.ecommerce.impressions.length > 0) {
                             dataLayer.push(event);
                         }
                     },
 
                     item_selector: '#lastviewed-widget .flex-viewport li',
 
                     imps: {
                         min_percentage_shown: 0.8,
                         buffer_flush_delay: 2,
 
                         event: enhancedCommerceHelper.prodImpressionEventDef,
 
                         item: function (idx, elem) {
                             var metadata = $(elem);
                             return {
                                 id: metadata.data("productid"),
                                 name: '',
                                 brand: metadata.data("brand"),
                                 category: '',
                                 dimension13: '',
                                 dimension14: '',
                                 dimension15: '',
                                 list: 'Reco Native Listing > ' + pageTypeMetadata.listing + ' > En Son İncelediğiniz Ürünler',
                                 position: idx + 1,
                             };
                         }
                     }
                 },
                 horizontalConstraintfunc: function ($elem) {
                     var container = $("#lastviewed-widget .flex-viewport");
                     var visibleWidth = container.width() + container.offset().left;
                     return $elem.offset().left + $elem.width() < visibleWidth;
                 }
             };
 
             $(window).on('scroll', registerLastViewedItemEvent);
             $(document).on('animationEnd:latestvieweditems', function () {
                 registerLastViewedItemEvent();
             });
 
             $(window).on('unload', enhancedCommerceHelper.flushBufferNow(lastViewedProdImpressions));
 
             function registerLastViewedItemEvent(e) {
                 var $lastViewedElems = $(lastViewedProdImpressions.options.item_selector);
 
                 if (lastViewedProdImpressions.buffered_items.length > 0 && e && e.type == "scroll") {
                     return $(window).off('scroll', registerLastViewedItemEvent);
                 } else if ($lastViewedElems.length > 0 && $lastViewedElems.prop("style").width != "") {
                     enhancedCommerceHelper.registerImpressions($lastViewedElems, lastViewedProdImpressions);
                 }
             }
         }
 
         trackLastViewedProducts();
         $(document).on("click", ".latestviewitems li", function(){
             enhancedCommerceHelper.productClickNativeRecommendation($(this), 'Reco Native Listing > ' + pageTypeMetadata.listing + ' > En Son İncelediğiniz Ürünler')
         });
     })();
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    (function () {
         var pageTypeMetadata = enhancedCommerceHelper.getPageTypeMetadata();
         $("iframe").closest('.ps_sidebar-item').addClass("enhancedVideo");
 
         trackImpressions();
 
         function trackImpressions() {
 
             var listImpressions = {
                 impressions_count: 0,
                 impressions_sent: {},
                 buffered_items: [],
                 flush_buffer_at: 0,
                 options: {
                     push: function (event) {
                         if (event.ecommerce.promoView.promotions.length > 0) {
                             dataLayer.push(event);
                         }
                     },
 
                     item_selector: '.longblocks,.shortblocks,.ps_sidebar-item,.ps_sidebar-item',
 
                     imps: {
                         min_percentage_shown: 0.8,
                         buffer_flush_delay: 2,
 
                         event: enhancedCommerceHelper.promoImpressionEventDef,
 
                         item: function (idx, elem) {
 
                             var anchor = $(elem).find("a");
                             var position = 0;
                             var name = '';
                             var id = '';
 
                             if ($(elem).hasClass('ps_sidebar-item')) {
                                 if (anchor.length > 0) {
                                     name = "PS-RHS|" + anchor.attr('title');
                                     id = name + "|" + anchor.attr('href');
                                 }
                                 position = $(elem).index() - $(elem).prevAll(".enhancedVideo").length + 1;
                             }
                             else if ($(elem).hasClass('longblocks') || $(elem).hasClass('shortblocks')) {
                                 var href = anchor.prop("href");
                                 var regexGroup = null;
                                 if (href.indexOf('kampanya') > -1) {
                                     regexGroup = href.match(/kampanya\/liste\/(\d+)/);
                                     name = "PS|" + anchor.find(".mh_promotion_slogan").text();
                                 }
                                 else if (href.indexOf('markalar') > -1) {
                                     regexGroup = href.match(/markalar\/0\/(\d+)/);
                                     name = "Sezon|" + anchor.find(".mh_promotion_slogan").text();
                                 }
                                 else if (href.indexOf('liste?') > -1) {
                                     regexGroup = href.match(/(\d+)\/liste/);
                                     name = "Sezon|" + anchor.find(".mh_promotion_slogan").text();
                                 }
 
                                 if (regexGroup != null) {
                                     var campaignId = regexGroup[1];
                                     id = name + "|" + campaignId;
 
                                     if ($(elem).hasClass("longblocks")) {
                                         position = $(elem).index() + 1;
                                     } else {
                                         position = $(".longblocks").length + $(elem).parent().index();
                                     }
                                 }
                             }
 
                             return {
                                 id: id,
                                 name: name,
                                 position: pageTypeMetadata.listing + "|" + position,
                             };
 
                         }
                     }
                 }
             };
 
             $(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 
             if (window.onbeforeunload) {
                 $(window).on('onbeforeunload', function () { enhancedCommerceHelper.flushBufferNow(listImpressions) });
             } else {
                 $(window).on('beforeunload', function () { enhancedCommerceHelper.flushBufferNow(listImpressions) });
             }
 
             function onScroll() {
                 var $listElems = $(listImpressions.options.item_selector).not('.enhancedVideo');
                 enhancedCommerceHelper.registerImpressions($listElems, listImpressions);
             }
         }
 
         $(".container").on('click', '.mh_promotion_container', function PSProductListProductClickEvent() {
             var anchor = $(this).find("a");
             var name = '';
             var id = '';
             var position = 0;
             var positionPrefix = pageTypeMetadata.listing;
 
             if ($(this).hasClass('longblocks') || $(this).hasClass('shortblocks')) {
                 name = "PS|" + anchor.attr('data-campaignname');
                 id = name + "|" + anchor.attr('data-campaignid') + "|" + anchor.attr('data-campaignintegrationcode');
                 position = anchor.attr('data-position');
             }
             else {
                 if (anchor.length > 0) {
                     name = "PS-RHS|" + anchor.attr('title');
                     id = name + "|" + anchor.attr('href');
                 } 
 
                 position = $(this).parent().index() - $(this).parent().prevAll(".enhancedVideo").length + 1;
                 positionPrefix = positionPrefix.replace('PS', 'PS-RHS');
             }
 
             dataLayer.push({
                 'ecommerce': {
                     'promoClick': {
                         'promotions': [
                             {
                                 'id': id,
                                 'name': name,
                                 'position': positionPrefix + "|" + position
                             }]
                     }
                 },
                 'Category': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
                 'Action': 'Browse',
                 'Label': 'Campaign Click',
                 'noninteraction': false,
                 'Value': 0,
                 'event': 'eeEvent'
             });
         });
     })();
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    (function () {
 
         var pageTypeMetadata = enhancedCommerceHelper.getPageTypeMetadata();
         var widgetName = "Öne Çıkan Ürünler";
         var containerId = "#sk-carousel-widget";
         var containerFinalWidth = 200;
 
         function trackHighlightProducts() {
             var opensInNewWindow = false;
             var specificListingAlias = "";
             if (window.location.pathname == "/siparis-basarili") {
                 containerId = "#sk-carousel-default";
                 opensInNewWindow = true;
                 widgetName = "İlginizi Çekebilecek Ürünler";
             }
             if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("arama") > -1) {
                 containerId = "#sk-carousel-default";
                 opensInNewWindow = true;
                 specificListingAlias = "Season No Result";
                 widgetName = "İlginizi Çekebilecek Ürünler";
             }
             if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya/arama") > -1) {
                 containerId = "#sk-carousel-default";
                 opensInNewWindow = true;
                 specificListingAlias = "PS No Result";
                 widgetName = "İlginizi Çekebilecek Ürünler";
             }
             if (window.location.pathname == "/kampanya/alisveris") {
                 containerId = "#sk-carousel-right";
                 opensInNewWindow = true;
                 containerFinalWidth = 150;
             }
             if(window.location.pathname.indexOf("liste") > -1  && window.location.pathname.indexOf("kampanya/liste") > -1) {
                 opensInNewWindow = true;
             }
             if (window.location.pathname.indexOf("marka") > -1) {
                 opensInNewWindow = true;
             }
 
 
 
             listingAlias = specificListingAlias == "" ? pageTypeMetadata.listing : specificListingAlias;
 
 
             if (opensInNewWindow) {
                 $(document).on("click", containerId + " li", function () {
                     enhancedCommerceHelper.productClickSkRecommendation($(this), 'Reco Shopkrowd Listing > ' + listingAlias + ' > ' + widgetName)
                 });
             }
 
             var timeoutCounter = 0;
             var highlightLoadTimer = setInterval(function () {
                 if ($(containerId).length > 0 && typeof $(containerId).data("flexslider") != "undefined") {
                     clearInterval(highlightLoadTimer); $(containerId).data("flexslider").vars["after"] = function () {
                         registerHighlightedItemEvent();
                     };
                 }
             }, 2000);
 
             var highlightProdImpressions = {
                 impressions_count: 0,
                 impressions_sent: {},
                 buffered_items: [],
                 flush_buffer_at: 0,
                 options: {
                     push: function (event) {
                         dataLayer.push(event);
                     },
 
                     item_selector: containerId + ' .flex-viewport li',
 
                     imps: {
                         min_percentage_shown: 0.8,
                         buffer_flush_delay: 2,
 
                         event: enhancedCommerceHelper.prodImpressionEventDef,
 
                         item: function (idx, elem) {
                             var prodId = '';
                             var anchor = $(elem).find("a");
                             var regexGroup = anchor.prop("href").match(/(\d+)\/detay/);
                             if (regexGroup == null) {
                                 regexGroup = anchor.prop("href").match(/kampanya\/detay\/(\d+)/);
                                 if (regexGroup.length == 2)
                                     prodId = regexGroup[1];
                             } else {
                                 if (regexGroup.length == 2)
                                     prodId = regexGroup[1];
                             }
 
                             return {
                                 id: prodId,
                                 name:  anchor.find(".brand").html() + " " + anchor.find(".name").html() + "|" + prodId,
                                 brand: anchor.find(".brand").html(),
                                 category: '',
                                 dimension13: '',
                                 dimension14: '',
                                 dimension15: '',
                                 list: 'Reco Shopkrowd Listing > ' + listingAlias + ' > ' + widgetName,
                                 position: idx + 1,
                             };
                         }
                     }
                 },
                 horizontalConstraintfunc: function ($elem) {
                     var container = $(containerId + " .flex-viewport");
                     var visibleWidth = container.width() + container.offset().left;
                     return $elem.offset().left + $elem.width() < visibleWidth;
                 }
             };
 
             $(window).on('scroll', registerHighlightedItemEvent);
 
             function registerHighlightedItemEvent(e) {
                 var $highlightElems = $(highlightProdImpressions.options.item_selector);
 
                 if (highlightProdImpressions.buffered_items.length > 0 && e && e.type == "scroll") {
                     return $(window).off('scroll', registerHighlightedItemEvent);
                 } else if ($highlightElems.length > 0 && $highlightElems.prop("style").width != "") {
                     enhancedCommerceHelper.registerImpressions($highlightElems, highlightProdImpressions);
                 }
             }
         }
 
         $('#quickview-modal').on('show.bs.modal', function (e) {
             if ($(e.relatedTarget).length == 0) {
                 $(document).on("modalLoaded", modalLoadedEnhancedEvent);
             }
         })
 
         var modalLoadedEnhancedEvent = function (e, productId) {
             if (!psNativeModalActive) {
                 $(document).off("modalLoaded", modalLoadedEnhancedEvent);
                 enhancedCommerceHelper.productClickSkRecommendation(null, 'Reco Shopkrowd Listing > ' + pageTypeMetadata.listing + ' > ' + widgetName, productId);
             }
         }
 
 
 
         trackHighlightProducts();
     })();
   </script>

   <script async="">
    $(document).ready(function () {
         var pageType2 = { page2: "VisilabsEvamUserSegmentEvent" }
         function getVisilabsEvamUserSegmentEvent(vl) {
             
     if(EventDataContext.User.IsLoggedIn)
     {
         vl.AddParameter('OM.exVisitorID', EventDataContext.User.UserMailingGuid);
     }
 
     if( EventDataContext.User.Gender==1)
     {
         vl.AddParameter('OM.gn', 'male');
     }
     else
     {
         vl.AddParameter('OM.gn', 'female');
     }
 
     vl.AddParameter('OM.arck', EventDataContext.User.RandomCookie)
 
     if (window.location.href == "http://www.morhipo.com/" || window.location.href == "https://www.morhipo.com/")
     {
         vl.AddParameter('OM.custom3', '');
     }
 
 
     vl.AddParameter('OM.vchannel', 'web');
 
 
 
 
         }
     });
   </script>
